<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Forum Energy Plc. 
(&#8220;FEP&#8221;)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">We currently own 18.42% of FEP. FEP was established through the
consolidation in 2005 of the Philippine assets of FEC Resources, Inc. of Canada,
and Sterling Energy Plc of the UK, into one corporate entity.&#160;&#160;The 
current holdings of FEP are based mainly in the Philippines and 
include:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt">
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new 
roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; DISPLAY: inline" face="Symbol, 
serif">&#183;&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">70% interest in Service Contract 72 Reed Bank (SC 72), an 
offshore license which contains the Sampaguita Gas Field as well as several 
additional oil and gas leshare;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt">
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new 
roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; DISPLAY: inline" face="Symbol, 
serif">&#183;&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">66.7% interest in Service Contract 40 North Cebu (SC 40), an 
onshore and offshore license which contains the onshore Libertad Gas Field and 
Maya discovery and several other prospects;&#160;&#160;and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new 
roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; DISPLAY: inline" face="Symbol, 
serif">&#183;&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">2.27% interest in Service Contract 14C1 Galoc (SC 14C1 Galoc), 
an offshore license which contains the producing Galoc Field.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">At the annual general meeting of Forum Energy on June 17, 2015,
the shareholders passed resolutions which approved the delisting of Forum Energy
from the London Stock Exchange and the conversion of FEP from a public company 
to a private company.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">In connection with the delisting,
FEP and Philex Petroleum announced an offer by Philex Petroleum to acquire the 
minority interests in FEP's Ordinary Shares not held by First Pacific Company 
Limited, Asia Link B.V., Philex Mining Corporation, FEC Resources Inc. and its 
nominee Ferlim Nominees Limited, and FEP shareholders in restricted 
jurisdictions for a cash consideration of 20 pence per Ordinary Share 
("Offer").&#160;&#160;A total of 2,383,777 shares were purchased by Philex 
Petroleum representing 6.71 per cent of FEP.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; 
DISPLAY: inline">SC 72 Reed Bank (formerly </font><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: 
bold; DISPLAY: inline">previously </font><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; 
DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: 
inline">Geophysical Survey and Exploration Contract No. 101</font><font 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"> 
(&#8220;</font><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: 
inline">GSEC101))</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The SC72 Reed Bank concession is located in the West Philippine
Sea west of Palawan Island.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The license was awarded to Sterling Energy Plc in June 2002. 
Exploration in the area began in 1970 and in 1976 gas was discovered following 
the drilling of a well.&#160;&#160;In total, four (4) wells have been drilled to
date, all located at the south west end of the license.&#160;&#160;Two (2) of 
the wells tested gas at rates of 3.6 mmcf/d and 3.2 mmcf/d.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In 2003, Sterling reprocessed 250 km of 2D seismic and 
completed a feasibility study on a GTL&#160;&#160;(gas-to-liquid) development 
scenario for the gas field.&#160;&#160;The seismic work and the GTL study 
fulfilled the initial work commitments on the concession and Sterling was 
granted a twelve (12) month extension in June 2004.&#160;&#160;In 2005, Forum 
acquired new 250 square kilometers of new 3D seismic data over the license area 
fulfilling its work commitments required under the twelve (12) month 
extension.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In September 2006, results of the interpretation of the 3D 
seismic program at the Sampaguita gas discovery indicated a significant gas 
accumulation.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">In 2008,&#160;&#160;FEP finalized
farm-out of a 30% interest in the license to a local partner Monte Oro Resources
&amp; Energy, Inc. (Monte Oro) in which FEP benefited from an immediate cash 
payment of $1.7million, securing Monte Oro&#8217;s involvement and thereby 
qualifying the Joint Venture for the Filipino Participation Incentive Allowance 
(FPIA) which entitles the Company to 7.5% of gross revenues, prior to sharing 
revenues with the government.</font></div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffd700">&#160;</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">In February 2010, the GSEC101 exploration license was converted
into Service Contract 72. The area of the block was reduced from 10,360 Km2 to 
8,800 Km2 as part of this conversion.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">In the first quarter of 2011, Forum completed 565 Km2 of 3D 
seismic acquisition over the Sampaguita Gas Field and 2,202 Line-Km of 2D 
seismic data was also acquired over the block in order to further define 
additional leshare.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">The interpretation of the surveys was carried out by 
Weatherford Petroleum Consultants 
(&#8220;Weatherford&#8221;).&#160;&#160;Weatherford&#8217;s report identified a 
number of drilling locations.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline"><a 
href="#TableofContents">Table of Contents</a></font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-
FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">15</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">FEP was planning the execution of the second sub-phase work 
program at SC72 which was expected to involve the drilling of up to two wells 
before August 14, 2013.&#160;&#160;On January 17, 2013 FEP announced that it had
applied for an extension to the second-sub phase of SC72 from the Philippine 
Department of Energy.&#160;&#160;On January 25, 2013 FEP announced that it was 
granted an extension until August 14, 2015 to complete the second sub-phase of 
SC72.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">SC 72 is located in an area which is subject to a maritime 
dispute between the Chinese and the Philippine governments. There are 
discussions being held to try and find a commercial solution but any such 
commercial solution would require the full support of the Philippine 
government.&#160;&#160;&#160;Recognizing that the delay in implement the 
drilling programme were for reasons beyond the control of Forum Energy, the
Philippine Department of Energy extended the end date of Sub-Phase 2 from August
14, 2013 to August 14, 2016.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">On March 4, 2015 the Philippine Department of Energy granted a 
force majeure on SC72 because this contract area falls within the territorial 
disputed area of the West Philippine Sea which is the subject of an United 
Nations arbitration process between the Republic of Philippines and the 
People&#8217;s Republic of China.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Under the terms of the force majeure, all exploration work at 
SC72 is immediately suspended (effective from 15 December 2014) until the DOE 
notifies the Company that it may commence drilling.&#160;&#160;As a result, the 
second sub-phase of SC72 was put on hold until further notice.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">&#160;It is anticipated that the terms of the second sub-phase 
and all subsequent sub-phases will be extended by the term of the force 
majeure.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">On July12, 2016, the Permanent Court of Arbitration in the 
Hague ruled in favor of the Philippines against China over <font style="TEXT-
DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">territorial disputes</font> in the South
China Sea. China has rejected the ruling. It is uncertain whether this ruling 
will resolve the dispute between the parties.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">FEP is also continuing to discuss potential partnerships with 
regards to SC72 to assist and augment in the successful acceleration of the 
development of the project.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">SC 40 North Cebu</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">FEP holds a 66.7% interest in the SC 40 (Cebu) contract area is
located in the Visayan Basin in the central part of the Philippines 
archipelago.&#160;&#160;The license area covers the northern area of Cebu Island
and the adjacent offshore areas in the Central Ta&#241;on Strait and Visayan 
Sea.&#160;&#160;Since 1994, a total of fifteen (15) wells have been drilled 
offshore in the Visayan Basin, thirteen (13) of these on the acreage covered by 
SC 40 (Cebu).</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Libertad Gas Field is situated within SC40.&#160;&#160;The 
field was discovered in the late 1950's, but was not developed.&#160;&#160;In 
1993, a testing program was carried out on two (2) wells and during 1994 and 
1995, five (5) additional wells were drilled on Libertad.&#160;&#160;One of 
these wells tested gas and subsequently was completed as a gas 
producer.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In 2004, FEP carried out a feasibility study to determine the 
most commercially viable option for the development of the Libertad Gas 
Field.&#160;&#160;The results of this work recommended a development plan using 
three (3) GTE generators, with a maximum of 3.0 MW.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">During December 2005, the 
Department of Energy formally granted a Declaration of Commerciality for the 
development of the onshore Libertad Gas Field.&#160;&#160;The Declaration of 
Commerciality allowed the retention of the portion of SC40 which contains all 
the currently identified prospects and discoveries.</font></div>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">During 2009 the Department of Energy approved the Gas Sale 
&amp; Purchase Agreement in respect of the development of the Libertad Gas Field
for a 1 MW gas turbine power plant.&#160;&#160;In February 2012, commercial 
production at the Libertad Field commenced and, as at 31 December 2013, the 
field has produced 144 million cubic feet of gas gross. However these revenues 
are not material to FEP&#8217;s cash flow. Having received a resource assessment
from Petroleum Geo-Services Asia Pacific Pte Ltd (PGS), an independent competent
person, on 19 February 2013 the investment in SC40 was impaired&#160;&#160;in 
2012 by US$25.4 million to US$3.25 million. An important factor in this 
assessment was that third parties had experienced a dry hole while drilling 
within the Ta&#241;on Straits which significantly reduced the likelihood of 
commercially viable hydrocarbon deposit in the offshore part of
SC40.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">SC 14C1 Galoc</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">FEP&#8217;s largest producing asset is the Galoc oil field<font
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>located offshore northwest
Palawan&#160;&#160;and has an area of 163 square kilometres and contains the 
Galoc oil field which was first put in production in 2008.&#160;&#160;Production
from the Galoc development reached 1.7 million barrels gross in 2013. FEP has a 
2.27% interest in the field and received US$2.1 million after deduction of share
of operating costs from crude sales from the field during the year. The second 
phase of development was completed in November 2013 with the drilling of two 
additional production wells.&#160;&#160;Total oil production from the four wells
was&#160;&#160;2.8 million barrels in 2014 at and achieved an average selling 
price of $105.80 per barrel. FEP secured US$2.58 million of financing from BNP 
Paribas in 2012 to help fund its share of development costs for this phase of 
the project <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; DISPLAY: inline">, </font>which was 
repaid in June 2014. In 2015 production from the Galoc field was 2.43 million 
barrels which achieved an average selling price of $53.8 per 
barrel.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">FEP anticipates lower revenues from the Galoc oil field in 2016
due to lower oil prices and a decline in production.&#160;&#160;Gross production
is forecast to decrease 2016.&#160;&#160;Further development of the Galoc field 
has been deferred until market conditions for oil improve.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline"><a 
href="#TableofContents">Table of Contents</a></font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-
FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">16</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Basic Petroleum &amp; Minerals Inc. 
(&#8220;BPMI&#8221;)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In May 2005, FEP entered into an agreement with Philippines-
based Basic Consolidated Inc. (&#8220;BCI&#8221;), whereby the parties agreed to
work under an exclusivity period towards finalizing the purchase by FEP of 
BCI&#8217;s petroleum interests in the Philippines, held through a wholly-owned 
subsidiary, BPMI. This culminated in February 2006 with the signing of a Share 
Purchase Agreement whereby FEP agreed to acquire 100% of BPMI in exchange for 
933,759 shares of FEP and deferred consideration.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The acquisition was approved by BCI shareholders at the 
company&#8217;s Annual General Meeting on March 29, 2006.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">BPMI assets included interests in nine (9) Philippine offshore 
fields, specifically the Galoc Field (2.27% participating interest) which 
commenced production in the fourth quarter 2008 and is currently in full 
production with 2.5 million barrels gross produced in 2009, and 2.69 million 
barrels gross in 2010. FEP received net revenues of $0.8 million in 2010 and 
2009.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">FEP also had nominal production from the SC6/14 Nido/Matinloc 
fields, which are contained within this block.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Previously, FEP also reported that its interest in the West 
Linepacan oil discovery was farmed-out for a 2.275% interest carried through 
development.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">On May 10 2011, FEP announced that it had come to a settlement 
with Basic Energy Corporation ("BEC") in relation to certain of its service
contracts in the NW Palawan area, offshore Philippines.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In the course of an arbitration process, on 10 May 2011, BEC 
and FEP signed a settlement agreement (the "Agreement") in relation to disputes 
relating to BEC's share in the historical cost recoveries arising from Service 
Contract 14 A and B (Nido-Matinloc Blocks), Service Contract 14-C (Galoc Block),
and other blocks of Service Contract 14 and Service Contract 6, pursuant to the 
Sale and Purchase Agreement executed by BEC and FEP on 3 April 2006 (the 
"SPA").</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In February 2012, FEP announced that the settlement agreement 
was not completed because not all required third party consents were obtained 
within the agreed timeframe resulting in the process going into 
arbitration.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">On June 21, 2012 FEP has disclosed that FEP and BEC have agreed
to a settlement under which FEP shall pay BEC the amount of $2,400,000, which is
the remaining balance of a $10,000,000 payment stipulated in the Sales and 
Purchase Agreement, plus an additional $2,000,000 with $1,000,000 of the 
$2,000,000 paid in December 2012 and the balance of the $2,000,000 paid in 
December 2013.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Metalore Mining Corp.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">MMC commenced preliminary mining operations at the beginning of
October 2005, with iron ore extraction mainly being recovered as strewn boulders
and debris recovered from routing of the mine access roshare leading to the main
iron ore body.&#160;&#160;As of March, 2006, Metalore had successfully completed
and shipped its first iron ore contract.&#160;&#160;Difficulties were 
encountered prior to this with overburdens of pyrites, where iron ore had been 
anticipated, and with environmental compliance.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><br>
<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">Mining operations were suspended in September 2006 because of problems 
caused by six (6) typhoons which hit the area in a three (3) month period and 
due to intervention by the local government of the Province of Bulacan who are 
in dispute with the central government (DENR) about who has jurisdiction over
the mining operations.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Metalore also decided to suspend mining operations under the 
Small Scale Mining Permits because of the limitations on equipment, namely the 
maximum of two (2) heavy excavators/bulldozers per 20 hectares.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Metalore has filed an application for an Exploration Permit 
over a total of 841 hectares which includes the small scale mining areas in 
which we were previously operating.&#160;&#160;Metalore management&#160; 
believed this would be approved after the May 2007 political elections 
and&#160;an MPSA would be granted, which is the relevant permit for large scale 
mining.&#160;&#160;To date there has been no further developments and Metalore 
operations continue to be abandoned.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">MPSA148 (Philex Gold Joint 
Venture)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The surface investigation and limited diamond drilling that 
started in mid-2005 have identified gold-bearing jasperoid horizons in two (2) 
prospects, Lascogon and Danao, Philippines.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Starting in July 2006, some 3,000 meters of reverse circulation
(RC) drilling over a 30 hectare (approx. 75 acres) area was done covering four 
(4) prospects.&#160;&#160;To date, we have spent in excess of $1,000,000 
evaluating the property.&#160;&#160;Most of the effort has focused on the 
southern portion of the holding and has encountered numerous positive shows of 
gold and copper, but not in sufficient quantities to warrant entering commercial
production.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In 2007, further trenching, drilling, sampling and assays were 
conducted &#160;on MPSA 148. These were done initially on the Lascogon and Danua
areas, then later, surveying, drilling and sampling on the Nabago prospective 
area.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Exploration during fiscal 2009 on the Lascogon Project was 
limited to trenching activities as recommended by project consultant IRES to 
provide additional basis for resource estimation. Limited work was completed on 
the property during fiscal 2010.</font></div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">

href="#TableofContents">Table of Contents</a></font></div>

</div>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">We received a technical report in respect of the Lascogon 
Project in 2010 prepared by Mr. Dexter S. Ferriera (a senior geostatistician and
mining engineer at Independent Resource Estimation or IRES) in accordance with 
National Instrument 43-101 <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: 
inline">Standards of Disclosure for Mineral Projects</font>. We evaluated the 
technical report and determined that the work completed on the Lascogon Project 
to date did not determine an economically viable gold reserve. Accordingly, we 
have fully written down our investment in Lascogon.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In May 2012, we received a capital call from Lascogon Mining in
the amount of 100 million Philippine Pesos or approximately 
$2,400,000.&#160;&#160;The capital call was made to address Lascogon 
Mining&#8217;s current deficit and to fund the upcoming work program and 
exploration budget.&#160;&#160;We were given until December 21, 2012 to forward 
the requested funds or have our 40% interest diluted to 1.08%.&#160;&#160;We did
not forward funds and therefore our interest in Lascogon Mining was diluted to 
1.08 %.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The current mining exploration phase of the MPSA expired in 
January 2014.&#160;&#160;The decision by the mining regulator in 2015 to decline
the granting of an extension has been appealed however it is uncertain when the 
result of this appeal will be known nor is the outcome certain. .</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">C.&#160;&#160;Organizational Structure</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">We are part of a group of companies with our parent company 
being Philex Petroleum Corporation and the ultimate parent company of our group 
of companies is Philex Mining Corporation. We have no subsidiaries.</font></div>
<br>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt;

0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;

few years, and as a result, our ability to continue as a going concern is 
dependent on achieving profitable operations and/or upon obtaining additional 
financing.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

with IFRS as issued by the IASB, which are&#160;&#160;different from US GAAP 
(refer to the Auditors&#8217; Report dated August 30, 2016).</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

DISPLAY: inline"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; DISPLAY: inline">The Company is 
exposed to foreign currency fluctuations for general and administrative 
transactions denominated in Canadian Dollars. The majority of the 
Company&#8217;s cash is kept in U.S. dollars.&#160;&#160;&#160;Cash held in 
Canadian dollars&#160;&#160;is subject to exchange rate fluctuations between the
Canadian dollars and the U.S. dollars</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY: Times New

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

December 31, 2015 versus December 31, 2014</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Our consolidated accounts show income for the year ended 
December 31, 2015 of $340,909 or $0.00 per share, versus a loss of $289,875 or 
$(0.00) per share for the year ended December 31, 2014.&#160;&#160;During the 
year ended December 31, 2015, we sold 2,000,000 shares of Forum Energy and 
recorded a gain of $637,902 which was the reason we reported income. General and
Administration expenses were $297,041 for the year ended December 31, 2015 
versus $289,980 for the same period in 2014. We recorded amortization of $365 
for the year ended December 31, 2015 versus $522 for the same period in 
2014.&#160;&#160;For the year ended December 31, 2015 foreign exchange loss was 
$5,684 versus a loss of $2,105 for the year ended December 31, 
2014.</font></div>

</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Interest income was $48 for the year ended December 31, 2015 
versus $105 for the previous year. The difference was a result of the interest 
earned on the higher cash balance in 2014.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline;

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline"><font
style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Capital 
Resources</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In order to fully earn a 40% interest in the joint venture with
Philex Gold Philippines Inc. (&#8220;PGPI&#8221;) on the Lascogon Project, we 
were required to fund a total of $1 million of the work program by October, 2006
which was completed. To maintain our 40% interest, we were required to pay for 
40% of the ongoing work program or our position would be diluted.&#160;&#160;In 
May 2012, we received a capital call from Lascogon Mining in the amount of 100 
million Philippine Pesos or approximately $2,400,000.&#160;&#160;The capital 
call was made to address Lascogon Mining&#8217;s current deficit and to fund the
upcoming work program and exploration budget.&#160;&#160;We were given until 
December 21, 2012 to forward the requested funds or have our 40% interest 
diluted to 1.08%.&#160;&#160;We did not forward funds and therefore our interest
in Lascogon Mining was diluted to 1.08 %.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">We currently own 35% of Metalore, 1.08% of Lascogon and 18.42% 
of FEP. All but FEP require us to fund our share of any work programs in order 
to maintain our current equity share in each company. If FEP is required to 
raise additional funds through equity issuances then we would have to purchase 
our proportionate share of these equity issuances to maintain our current equity
position.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Should we be unable to meet our share of the work programs then
our holdings would be diluted down accordingly.&#160;&#160;In 2007, we wrote off
our investment in Metalore and in 2010, we wrote off our investment in 
Lascogon.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">We anticipate that we will require additional funds for working
capital for the next twelve months from the date of this filing and we are 
evaluating options in order to raise the additional funds.&#160;&#160;We may be 
able to sell our FEP shares should the need arise. If we are unable to raise 
additional funds by way of selling our FEP shares in an orderly transaction, 
there is substantial doubt that we will be able to continue as a going 
concern.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline"><font 
style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Off-Balance Sheet 
Arrangements</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">We have no off-balance sheet arrangements.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">Contractual Obligations</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">None</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Critical Accounting Policies and 
Estimates</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Basis of preparation and
accounting policies</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Company has prepared its consolidated financial statements 
in accordance with IFRS as issued by the International Accounting Standards 
Board (&#8220;IASB&#8221;). IFRS represents standards and interpretations 
approved by the IASB and are comprised of IFRS, International Accounting 
Standards (&#8220;IAS&#8217;s&#8221;), and interpretations issued by the IFRS 
Interpretations Committee (&#8220;IFRIC&#8217;s&#8221;) and the former Standing 
Interpretations Committee (&#8220;SIC&#8217;s&#8221;).. The consolidated 
financial statements have been prepared in accordance with IFRS standards and 
interpretations effective as of December 31, 2015.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt;

href="#TableofContents">Table of Contents</a></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Critical Accounting Estimates</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The preparation of financial statements requires management to 
make certain judgments and estimates.&#160;&#160;Changes in these judgments and 
estimates could have a material impact on our reported financial result and 
financial condition.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Company makes estimates and assumptions about the future 
that affect the reported amounts of assets and liabilities. Estimates and 
judgments are continually evaluated based on historical experience and other 
factors, including expectations of future events that are believed to be 
reasonable under the circumstances. In the future, actual experience may differ 
from these estimates and assumptions.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">Determination of natural resource reserves and natural 
resources estimates</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The required process of estimating reserves of natural 
resources is critical to several accounting estimates that appear in our 
financial disclosures.&#160;&#160;It requires significant judgments based on 
available geological, geophysical, engineering and economic 
data.&#160;&#160;These estimates may change substantially as data from ongoing 
development and production activities becomes available, and as economic 
conditions impacting oil and natural gas prices, operating costs, and royalty 
burdens change.&#160;&#160;Reserve estimates impact net income through depletion
and the application of an impairment test.&#160;&#160;Revisions or changes in 
the reserve estimates can have either a positive or negative impact on net
income.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">Deferred tax assets and liabilities</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Significant judgment is required in determining the provision 
for income taxes. There are many transactions and calculations undertaken during
the ordinary course of business for which the ultimate tax determination is 
uncertain. We recognize liabilities and contingencies for anticipated tax audit 
issues based on our current understanding of the tax law. For matters where it 
is probable that an adjustment will be made, we record our best estimate of the 
tax liability including the related interest and penalties in the current tax 
provision. We believe we have adequately provided for the probable outcome of 
these matters; however, the final outcome may result in a materially different 
outcome than the amount included in the tax liabilities.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">Determination of significant influence over 
investments</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Judgment is required to determine whether significant influence
exists over companies in which we hold investments. Significant influence is 
presumed to exist if an entity holds 20&#160;per cent or more of the voting 
power of the investee unless it can be clearly demonstrated that this is not the
case. Conversely, if the entity holds less than 20&#160;per cent of the voting 
power of the investee, it is presumed that the entity does not have significant 
influence, unless such influence can be clearly demonstrated. The existence of 
significant influence by an entity is usually evidenced by one or more of the 
following:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: 
inline">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;rep
resentation on the board of directors or equivalent governing body of the 
investee;</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: 
inline">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;par
ticipation in policy-making processes, including participation in decisions 
about dividends or other<font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 
12pt"></font>distributions;</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: 
inline">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;mat
erial transactions between the entity and its investee;</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: 
inline">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;int
erchange of managerial personnel; or</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: 
inline">(e)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;pro
vision of essential technical information.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">We determined that, despite having its ownership of FEP reduced
to 18.42% of the outstanding shares of FEP by way of a sale of a portion of its 
shareholdings during the year ended December 31, 2015,&#160;we still maintained 
significant influence over the operations of FEP by virtue of our CEO and CFO 
holding a seat on the board of FEP as well being the Finance Director of 
FEP.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline"><font 
style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Lascogon Contingent 
Consideration</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">There were 30,000,000 common shares of ours issued into escrow 
which are to be awarded to the vendor of the investment in Lascogon upon the 
declaration of commerciality as full and final consideration for the investment;
these shares are considered contingent consideration. These shares are to be 
released from escrow if the project is declared commercial and were deemed to 
have zero value when they were issued. Accordingly no liability has been 
recognized.&#160;&#160;At December 31, 2015 and at the date of this report, it 
is was not considered likely that a declaration of commerciality would take 
place.&#160;&#160;In February 2016, we paid the vendor of the investment $36,000
and by mutual consent the shares were canceled and returned to treasury pursuant
to a settlement agreement.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">Functional Currency</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">We evaluated our functional currency and determined that the 
United States Dollar was our functional currency.&#160;&#160;All accounts and 
transactions were converted into US dollars from the transition date to 
IFRS.&#160;&#160;We&#160;&#160;determined that the effective date of the change 
in functional currency under IFRS was March 11, 2003.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Share capital and investments were converted from January 1, 
2003 as a result of the conversion to IFRS.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Recent&#160;&#160;Accounting Related 
Pronouncements</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The following new standards, amendments and interpretations, 
which have not been early adopted in these financial statements, will or may 
have an effect on the Company&#8217;s future results and financial 
position</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 9 Financial 
Instruments</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 9, Financial Instruments (&#8220;IFRS 9&#8221;) was issued
by the IASB in its final version in July 2014, and will replace IAS 39, 
"Financial Instruments: Recognition and Measurement" (&#8220;IAS 39&#8221;). 
IFRS 9 replaces the multiple rules in IAS 39 with a single approach to determine
whether a financial asset is measured at amortized cost or fair value and a new 
mixed measurement model for debt instruments having only two categories: 
amortized cost and fair value. The approach in IFRS 9 is based on how an entity 
manages its financial instruments in the context of its business model and the 
contractual cash flow characteristics of the financial assets. The new standard 
also requires a single impairment method to be used, replacing the multiple 
impairment methods in IAS 39. IFRS 9 is effective for annual periods beginning 
on or after January 1, 2018.&#160;&#160;The Company anticipates that this 
standard will be adopted in the Company&#8217;s financial statements for the 
period beginning January 1, 2018, and has not yet considered the potential 
impact of the adoption of IFRS 9.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 15 Revenue from 
Contracts with Customers</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 15, Revenue from Contracts with Customers (&#8220;IFRS 
15&#8221;) will replace IAS 18, "Revenue", IAS 11 &#8221;Construction Contracts 
and certain revenue related interpretations. IFRS 15 establishes a new control-
based revenue recognition model, changes the basis for the determination of when
revenue is recognized and improves disclosures about revenue. IFRS 15 also 
includes more detailed guidance as to when to account separately for individual 
performance obligations in a multiple element arrangement. The IASB has deferred
the effective date of IFRS 15 to annual periods beginning on or after January 1,
2018 with early adoption permitted. The Company has not yet considered the 
potential impact of the adoption of IFRS 15.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 16 
Leases</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 16, Leases (&#8220;IFRS 16&#8221;) will replace IAS 17, 
"Leases". IFRS 16 eliminates the distinction between operating and finance 
leases and requires most leases to be recorded on the balance sheet for lessees 
under a single model unless the lease term is twelve months or less or the 
underlying asset has low value. IFRS 16 has an effective date for annual periods
beginning on or after January 1, 2019 with early adoption permitted if IFRS 15 
is also applied. The Company is assessing the impact, if any, the adoption of 
IFRS 16 will have on its financial statements.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new 
roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">There are no other IFRSs or IFRIC interpretations that are not 
yet effective that would be expected to have a material impact on the 
Company.</font></div>
</td>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Information About our Directors and 
Officers</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Mr. Paul Wallace Chairman, President, Chief 
Executive Officer, and Chief Financial Officer</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Mr. Paul Frederick Wallace is a Chartered Professional 
Accountant and member of the CPA Canada.&#160;&#160;&#160;He was appointed as 
the Chief Financial Officer of Hong Kong based First Pacific Company Limited 
from 1995 to 1997between 2003 and 2004 and between 2014 and 2015. &#160;He was 
appointed Group Finance Director to the Sanctuary Group plc between 2005 and 
2008. Mr. Wallace was Chief Executive Officer of Blue Ocean Wireless Limited 
between 2009 and 2011, and a Non-Executive Director of JPMorgan Global Emerging 
Markets Income Trust Plc between 2010 and 2015.&#160;&#160;He is also the 
Finance Director of FEP, a Director of Pitkin Petroleum and Head of Finance of 
Goodman Fielder Pty Limited.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Mr. Claro Ramirez</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Mr. Ramirez is a resident of Richmond, British Columbia, Canada
and has served as Senior Vice President of Philippine Long Distance Telephone 
Company (&#8220;PLDT&#8221;) for the last eleven years.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Mr. Lyle Brown</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Mr. Brown is a resident of Vancouver, British Columbia, 
Canada.&#160;&#160;He is a Chartered Professional Accountant 
and&#160;&#160;Partner of Culver &amp; Co., an accounting firm, since 
1991.&#160;&#160;&#160;Mr. Brown is also a director of Northern Lion Gold Corp 
and New World Resources Corp which are both listed on the TSX-V and Frankfurt 
stock exchanges.&#160;&#160;Mr. Brown is also a director of Nano One Materials 
Corp which is listed on the TSX-V.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">None of our directors and/or executive officers, or those 
persons to be appointed, have been the subject of any order, judgment, or decree
of any governmental agency or administrator, or of any court of competent 
jurisdiction, revoking or suspending for cause any license, permit or other 
authority of such person or of any corporation of which he or she is a director 
and/or executive officer, to engage in the securities business or in the sale of
a particular security or temporarily or permanently restraining or enjoining any
such person or any corporation of which he or she is an officer or director from
engaging in or continuing any conduct, practice, or employment in connection 
with the purchase or sale of securities, or convicting such person of any felony
or misdemeanor involving a security, or any aspect of the securities business, 
or of theft, or of any felony.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

or more directors or executive officers, pursuant to which he or she was 
selected as a Director or Executive Officer.&#160;&#160;There are no family 
relationships between any two (2) or more of our directors or executive 
officers.</font></div>

</div>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">Options to Purchase Our Securities.</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Options to purchase securities from us are granted to 
directors, officers and employees on terms and conditions acceptable to the 
relevant regulatory authorities.&#160;&#160;We adopted a formal stock option 
plan on June 19, 2000.&#160;&#160;There were no stock options outstanding on 
December 31, 2015 and none were issued or exercised in 2015 or 
2014.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">C.&#160;&#160;Board Practices</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">We have an Audit Committee, a Compensation Committee and a 
Corporate Governance Committee.&#160;&#160;No committee members receive 
additional compensation for serving on a committee and all committee members 
serve for a one year term.&#160;&#160;All board members are elected at our 
Annual General Meeting to serve for one year or until their successor is 
appointed.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Audit 
Committee</font>. The Audit Committee oversees the retention, performance and 
compensation of our independent auditors, and the establishment and oversight of
our systems of internal accounting and auditing control.&#160;&#160;Members of 
the Audit Committee in 2015 Lyle Brown, Claro Ramirez, and Paul 
Wallace.&#160;&#160;New members of our Audit Committee for 2016 
will&#160;&#160;be appointed following our Annual and General Meeting of 
Shareholders.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Compensation 
Committee</font>. The Compensation Committee reviews and makes recommendations 
to our Board concerning the terms of the compensation packages provided to our 
senior executive officers, including salary, bonus and awards under our stock 
option plan and any other compensation plans that we may adopt in the 
future.&#160;&#160;Members of the Compensation Committee in 2015 were Paul 
Wallace, Carlo Pablo until he resigned in August 2015, and Riaz Sumar until he 
resigned in June 2015.&#160;&#160;Members of our Compensation Committee for 2016
will&#160;&#160;be appointed following our Annual and General Meeting of 
Shareholders.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Corporate 
Governance Committee</font>. The Corporate Governance Committee meets with and 
discusses current disclosure issuances with our management personnel, directors,
and with both our Canadian and United States counsel, to report to our Board any
matters which should be the subject of either public disclosure or remedial 
action and to assist our Board in establishing reporting and disclosure 
procedures to ensure that we are in compliance with our disclosure and 
compliance obligations under applicable laws, rules and 
obligations.&#160;&#160;Members of our Corporate Governance Committee in 2015 
were Claro Ramirez, Lyle Brown, and Riaz Sumar until he resigned in June 
2015.&#160;&#160;Members of our Corporate Governance Committee for 2016 
will&#160;&#160;be appointed following our Annual and General Meeting of 
Shareholders,</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><br>
<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; 
DISPLAY: inline"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; TEXT-DECORATION: 
underline; DISPLAY: inline">D. </font><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">Employees</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">As of December 31, 2015, we had no employees.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">E.&#160;&#160;Share Ownership</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

DISPLAY: inline">The following table sets forth certain information as of August
3, 2016 regarding the ownership of our common stock by (i) each of our 
directors, (ii) each of our named executive officers, and (iii) all of our 
directors and executive officers as a group.&#160;&#160;Except as otherwise 
indicated, the address of each person identified below is c/o FEC Resources Inc,
203, 200 Barclay Parade S.W., Calgary, Alberta, T2P 4R5.&#160;&#160;We believe

and beneficial and that such persons have sole voting and investment power with 
respect to the shares indicated.&#160;&#160;Percentage of class in the following

conversion of various securities) / (total shares outstanding + shares issuable

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;

its parent company Philex Petroleum Corporation (&#8220;Philex&#8221;) for 21 
British pence per share. As a result of the sale of the shares, the Company 
recorded a gain on sale of $637,902.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Related party transactions are measured at exchange 
value.</font></div>
