<div style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">FEC RESOURCES INC.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">NOTES TO THE FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">December 31, 2015</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">(<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: 
inline">Stated in United States Dollars</font>)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<br>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Note 
3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<font style="TEXT-
DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Summary of Significant Accounting 
Policies</font> (continued)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; e)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: 
black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-
FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: 
underline; DISPLAY: inline">Earnings / Loss Per Share 
(continued)</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Diluted earnings/loss per common share is computed by dividing 
the net income or loss applicable to common shares by the sum of the weighted 
average number of common shares issued and outstanding and all additional common
shares that would have been outstanding, if potentially dilutive instruments 
were converted.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">There were no dilutive instruments (consisting of shares 
issuable on the exercise of options and warrants) outstanding during the years 
ended December 31, 2015, December 31, 2014 and December 31, 
2013.&#160;&#160;Accordingly, there is no difference in the amounts presented 
for basic and diluted loss per share.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; f)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: 
black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-
FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: 
underline; DISPLAY: inline">Financial Instruments</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Financial Assets</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Financial assets and liabilities are recognized when the 
Company becomes a party to the contractual provisions of the instrument. 
Financial assets are derecognized when the rights to receive cash flows from the
assets have expired or have been transferred and the Company has transferred 
substantially all risks and rewards of ownership.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Non-derivative financial assets that do not meet the definition
of loans and receivables are classified as available-for-sale and comprise 
principally the Company&#8217;s investments in entities not qualifying as 
subsidiaries or associates. Available-for-sale investments are carried at fair 
value with changes in fair value recognized in other comprehensive income/loss. 
If there is no quoted market price in an active market and fair value cannot be 
readily determined, then available-for sale investments are carried at 
cost.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Company has designated cash as loans and receivables, which
is measured at amortized cost.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Impairment on Financial Assets</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">At each reporting date the Company assesses whether there is 
any objective evidence that a financial asset or a group of financial assets is 
impaired. A financial asset or group of financial assets is deemed to be 
impaired, if, and only if, there is objective evidence of impairment as a result
of one or more events that has occurred after the initial recognition of the 
asset and that event has an impact on the estimated future cash flows of the 
financial asset or the group of financial assets.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">With the exception of equity instruments classified as 
available for sale, if, in a subsequent period, the amount of the impairment 
loss decreases and the decrease relates to an event occurring after the 
impairment was recognized; the previously recognized impairment loss is reversed
through profit or loss. On the date of impairment reversal, the carrying amount 
of the financial asset cannot exceed its amortized cost had impairment not been 
recognized.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

DISPLAY: inline">NOTES TO THE FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

DISPLAY: inline">December 31, 2015</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">(<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: 
inline">Stated in United States Dollars</font>)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
</div>
<br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Note 
3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<font style="TEXT-
DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Summary of Significant Accounting 
Policies</font> (continued)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;f)</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-
DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Financial Instruments 
(continued)</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Financial Liabilities</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Financial liabilities are classified as other financial 
liabilities, based on the purpose for which the liability was incurred, and 
comprise of trade payables and accrued liabilities. These liabilities are 
initially recognized at fair value net of any transaction costs directly 
attributable to the issuance of the instrument and subsequently carried at 
amortized cost using the effective interest rate method.&#160;&#160;This ensures
that any interest expense over the period to repayment is at a constant rate on 
the balance of the liability carried in the statement of financial position. 
Interest expense in this context includes initial transaction costs and premiums
payable on redemption, as well as any interest or coupon payable while the 
liability is outstanding. Trade and other payables represent liabilities for 
goods and services provided to the Company prior to the end of the period which 
are unpaid.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; g)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: 
black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-
FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: 
underline; DISPLAY: inline">Share capital</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Equity instruments are contracts that give a residual interest 
in the net assets of the Company. Financial instruments issued by the Company 
are classified as equity only to the extent that they do not meet the definition
of a financial liability or financial asset. The Company&#8217;s common shares 
are classified as equity instruments.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Incremental costs directly attributable to the issue of new 
shares or options are shown in equity as a deduction, net of tax, from the 
proceeds.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; h)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: 
black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-
FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: 
underline; DISPLAY: inline">Finance income and expenses</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Finance expense comprises interest expense on borrowings, 
accretion of the discount on provisions and impairment losses recognized on 
financial assets.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Interest income is recognized as it accrues in profit or loss, 
using the effective interest method.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Foreign currency gains and losses, reported under finance 
income and expenses, are reported on a net basis.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Note 
4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<font style="TEXT-
DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Standards, Amendments and 
Interpretations</font></font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">(<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: 
inline">Stated in United States Dollars</font>)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new 
roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Note 
4</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: 
inline">Standards, Amendments and Interpretations 
(continued)</font></font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The following new standards, amendments and interpretations, 
which have not been early adopted in these financial statements, will or may 
have an effect on the Company&#8217;s future results and financial 
position:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 9 Financial 
Instruments</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 9, Financial Instruments (&#8220;IFRS 9&#8221;) was issued
by the IASB in its final version in July 2014, and will replace IAS 39, 
"Financial Instruments: Recognition and Measurement" (&#8220;IAS 39&#8221;). 
IFRS 9 replaces the multiple rules in IAS 39 with a single approach to determine
whether a financial asset is measured at amortized cost or fair value and a new 
mixed measurement model for debt instruments having only two categories: 
amortized cost and fair value. The approach in IFRS 9 is based on how an entity 
manages its financial instruments in the context of its business model and the 
contractual cash flow characteristics of the financial assets. The new standard 
also requires a single impairment method to be used, replacing the multiple 
impairment methods in IAS 39. IFRS 9 is effective for annual periods beginning 
on or after January 1, 2018.&#160;&#160;The Company anticipates that this 
standard will be adopted in the Company&#8217;s financial statements for the 
period beginning January 1, 2018, and has not yet considered the potential 
impact of the adoption of IFRS 9.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 15 Revenue from 
Contracts with Customers</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 15, Revenue from Contracts with Customers (&#8220;IFRS 
15&#8221;) will replace IAS 18, "Revenue", IAS 11 &#8221;Construction Contracts 
and certain revenue related interpretations. IFRS 15 establishes a new control-
based revenue recognition model, changes the basis for the determination of when
revenue is recognized and improves disclosures about revenue. IFRS 15 also 
includes more detailed guidance as to when to account separately for individual 
performance obligations in a multiple element arrangement. The IASB has deferred
the effective date of IFRS 15 to annual periods beginning on or after January 1,
2018 with early adoption permitted. The Company has not yet considered the 
potential impact of the adoption of IFRS 15.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 16 
Leases</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">IFRS 16, Leases (&#8220;IFRS 16&#8221;) will replace IAS 17, 
"Leases". IFRS 16 eliminates the distinction between operating and finance 
leases and requires most leases to be recorded on the balance sheet for lessees 
under a single model unless the lease term is twelve months or less or the 
underlying asset has low value. IFRS 16 has an effective date for annual periods
beginning on or after January 1, 2019 with early adoption permitted if IFRS 15 
is also applied. The Company is assessing the impact, if any, the adoption of 
IFRS 16 will have on its financial statements.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

DISPLAY: inline">Note 
5&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: 
underline; DISPLAY: inline">Critical Accounting Estimates and 
Judgments</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Company makes estimates and assumptions about the future 
that affect the reported amounts of assets and liabilities. Estimates and 
judgments are continually evaluated based on historical experience and other 
factors, including expectations of future events that are believed to be 
reasonable under the circumstances. In the future, actual experience may differ 
from these estimates and assumptions.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The effect of a change in an accounting estimate is recognized 
prospectively by including it in comprehensive income/loss in the period of the
change, if the change affects that period only, or in the period of the change 
and future periods, if the change affects both.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;

policies that have the most significant risk of causing material adjustment to 
the carrying amounts of assets and liabilities recognized in the financial 
statements within the next financial year are discussed below:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new

<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 108pt">
<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">i)&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Lascogon Contingent Consideration &#8211; Note 8 
(iii)</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">There were 30,000,000 common shares of the Company issued into 
escrow which are to be awarded to Indexa Corp., the vendor of the investment in 
Lascogon, upon the declaration of commerciality of the mining project as full 
and final consideration for the investment; these shares are considered 
contingent consideration. These shares were to be released from escrow if the 
project was declared commercial and were deemed to have zero value when they 
were issued as the likelihood of the Lascogon being in a position to declare 
commerciality was remote. Accordingly no liability was 
recognized.&#160;&#160;Subsequent to year end, a settlement was reached whereby 
the shares were cancelled and returned to treasury for a payment of $36,000 to 
Indexa Corp.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE:

<td width="2702">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Deferred tax assets and liabilities</font></div>
</td>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Significant judgment is required in determining the provision 
for income taxes. There are many transactions and calculations undertaken during
the ordinary course of business for which the ultimate tax determination is 
uncertain. We recognize liabilities and contingencies for anticipated tax audit 
issues based on our current understanding of the tax law. For matters where it 
is probable that an adjustment will be made, we record our best estimate of the 
tax liability including the related interest and penalties in the current tax 
provision. We believe we have adequately provided for the probable outcome of 
these matters; however, the final outcome may result in a materially different 
outcome than the amount included in the tax liabilities.</font></div>

<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY:

</td>
<td width="2703">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Determination of natural resource reserves and natural 
resources estimates</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The required process of estimating reserves of natural 
resources is critical to several accounting estimates that appear in our 
financial disclosures.&#160;&#160;It requires significant judgments based on 
available geological, geophysical, engineering and economic 
data.&#160;&#160;These estimates may change substantially as data from ongoing 
development and production activities becomes available, and as economic 
conditions impacting oil and natural gas prices, operating costs, and royalty 
burdens change.&#160;&#160;Reserve estimates impact net income through depletion
and the application of an impairment test.&#160;&#160;Revisions or changes in 
the reserve estimates can have either a positive or negative impact on net 
income.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt;

daily bank deposit rates.</font></div>

<div align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;

18.42% (2014 &#8211; 24.05%).</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 81pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">During the year ended December 31, 2012, FEP wrote down 
$25,400,000 of its investment in Service Contract 40 &#8220;SC40&#8221; as a 
result of receiving a resource estimate from an independent 
consultant.&#160;&#160;The Company&#8217;s equity share of the losses incurred 
by FEP was in excess of the carrying value of the investment prior to recording 
the loss. However, in accordance with the guidance of IFRS, the Company 
discontinued recording losses once the carrying value of the equity investment 
was reduced to zero. As result, the Company&#8217;s investment in FEP was 
reduced to $Nil.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 81pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 81pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">At the annual general meeting of FEP on June 17, 2015, the 
shareholders passed resolutions which approved the delisting of FEP from the 
London Stock Exchange and the conversion of FEP from a public company to a 
private company.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 81pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">On November 16, 2015 the Company sold 2,000,000 FEP shares to 
its parent company Philex Petroleum Corporation (&#8220;Philex&#8221;) for 21 
British pence per share.&#160;&#160;As a result of the sale of the shares, the 
Company recorded a gain on sale of $637,902.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 81pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">At December 31, 2015, the Company held 6,550,200 shares of 
FEP.</font></div>

<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY:

</td>
<td width="2701">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Investment in Lascogon Mining Corporation 
(&#8220;Lascogon&#8221;)</font></div>
</td>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new

<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 94.5pt">
<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">30,000,000 common shares of the Company&#160;&#160;were issued 
into escrow, which were to be awarded to the vendor of the investment in 
Lascogon upon the declaration of commerciality as full and final consideration 
for the assignment of its rights to the Company, were considered contingent 
consideration and were to be recorded as an additional cost of the investment, 
at fair value, should Lascogon reach commerciality. Subsequent to year end, a 
settlement was reached whereby the shares were cancelled and returned to
treasury for a payment of $36,000.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 99pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In May 2012, the Company received a capital call from Lascogon 
in the amount of 100 million Philippine Pesos or approximately 
$2,400,000.&#160;&#160;The capital call was made to address Lascogon&#8217;s 
current deficit and to fund the upcoming work program and exploration 
budget.&#160;&#160;The Company was given until December 21, 2012 to forward the 
requested funds or have its 40% interest diluted to 1.08%.&#160;&#160;The 
Company did not forward funds and therefore its interest in Lascogon has been 
diluted to 1.08% with the result being that Lascogon was no longer considered an
associate of the Company as the Company no longer exerts significant influence. 
Upon the dilution of its interest in Lascogon, the investment was reclassified 
to an available for sale investment having a fair value of $Nil as at December 
31, 2014 and 2013.<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; DISPLAY: 
inline">&#160;</font>The current exploration phase under the Mineral Production 
Sharing Agreement (&#8220;MPSA&#8221;) expired in January 2014 and it remains 
uncertain whether a further 2 year extension will be granted.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 99pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; DISPLAY: inline">The 
Company&#8217;s cumulative cost in its investment in Lascogon is $2,635,254 
offset by equity share of losses totaling $27,640 and an impairment write-down 
of $2,607,614 leaving a carrying value of $Nil.</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; DISPLAY:

<td valign="bottom" width="1%" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid; TEXT-

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">As at December 31, 2015, the Company had estimated non-capital 
losses for Canadian tax purposes of $3,951,000 which may be carried forward to 
offset future years&#8217; taxable income.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

DISPLAY: inline">The potential benefit of these carry-forward non-capital losses
has not been recognized in these financial statements as it is not considered 
probable that sufficient future taxable profit will allow the deferred tax asset
to be recovered.</font></div>

<div style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">FEC RESOURCES INC.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">December 31, 2015</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">(<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY:

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Note 
13&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">Financial Instruments and Risk Management</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">The Company is exposed through its operations to the following 
financial risks:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new 
roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 90pt">
<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">-&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Market Risk</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new 
roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 90pt">
<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">-&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Credit Risk</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new 
roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 90pt">
<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">-&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" 
align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Liquidity Risk</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">In common with all other businesses, the Company is exposed to 
risks that arise from its use of financial instruments. This note describes the 
Company&#8217;s objectives, policies and processes for managing those risks and 
the methods used to measure them. Further quantitative information in respect of
these risks is presented throughout these financial statements.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">There have been no substantive changes in the Company&#8217;s 
exposure to financial instrument risks, its objectives, polices and processes 
for managing those risks or the methods used to measure them from previous years
unless otherwise stated in the note.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">General Objectives, Policies and Procedures</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Board of Directors has overall responsibility for the 
determination of the Company&#8217;s risk management objectives and policies 
and, whilst retaining ultimate responsibility for them, it has delegated the 
authority for designing and operating processes that ensure the effective 
implementation of the objectives and policies to the Company&#8217;s finance 
function. The Board of Directors receive quarterly reports from the 
Company&#8217;s Chief Financial Officer through which it reviews the 
effectiveness of the processes put in place and the appropriateness of the 
objectives and policies it sets.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The overall objective of the Board is to set policies that seek
to reduce risk as far as possible without unduly affecting the Company&#8217;s 
competitiveness and flexibility. Further details regarding these policies are 
set out below.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">a)</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Market Risk</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Market risk is the risk that the fair value of future cash 
flows of a financial instrument will fluctuate because of changes in market 
prices. Market prices are comprised of foreign currency risk, interest rate risk
and equity and commodity price risk.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Foreign currency exchange risk</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new 
roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 90pt">
<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: 
inline">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Company is exposed to foreign currency fluctuations for 
general and administrative transactions denominated in Canadian Dollars. The
majority of the Company&#8217;s cash is kept in U.S. dollars.&#160;&#160;As at 
December 31, 2015, the Company had an insignificant amount of cash denominated 
in Canadian dollars that was subject to exchange rate fluctuations between the 
Canadian dollar and the U.S. dollar. As at December 31, 2015, the Company held 
an insignificant amount of financial liabilities denominated in Canadian dollars
that would be subject to exchange rate fluctuations between Canadian dollars and
U.S. dollars.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">FEC RESOURCES INC.</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">NOTES TO THE FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">December 31, 2015</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">(<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: 
inline">Stated in United States Dollars</font>)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Note 
13&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<font style="TEXT-
DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Financial Instruments and Risk 
Management</font> (continued)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Interest Rate Risk</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Interest rate risk is the risk that the fair values and future 
cash flows of the Company will fluctuate because of changes in market interest 
rates. The Company is exposed to interest rate risk on its cash. The Company did
not have any borrowings outstanding as at December 31, 2015.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
72pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt"></font>Equity and 
Commodity Price Risk</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Equity risk is the uncertainty associated with the valuation of
assets arising from changes in equity markets.&#160;&#160;The Company is exposed
to this risk through its equity holdings. The investment in FEP is monitored by 
Management with decisions on sale taken at Board level.&#160;&#160;The Company 
is exposed to Commodity Price Risk as FEP is actively involved in exploration 
for oil and gas.&#160;&#160;A significant increase or decrease in commodity 
prices will likely have a resultant effect on the Company&#8217;s share 
price.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">b)</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Credit risk</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Company maintains cash deposits in one chartered Canadian 
bank which, from time to time, exceed the amount of depositors insurance 
available in each respective account.&#160;&#160;Management assesses the 
financial condition of this bank and believes that the possibility of any credit
loss is minimal.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">c)</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Liquidity risk</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Liquidity risk is the risk that the Company will not be able to
meet its obligations as they fall due.&#160;&#160;The Company does not generate 
cash from operations but rather, the Company will, from time to time, issue 
shares via equity placements, borrow funds from an affiliated company or 
undertake to sell a portion of its investment in the shares of FEP should it be 
necessary to raise funds. The Company manages liquidity by maintaining cash 
balances available to meet its anticipated operational needs. Liquidity 
requirements are managed based on expected cash flow to ensure that there is 
adequate capital to meet short-term and long-term obligations. The Company has 
in place a planning and budgeting process to help determine the funds required 
to support the Company&#8217;s normal operating requirements on an ongoing basis
and its growth plans. At December 31, 2015 the Company&#8217;s accounts payable 
and accrued liabilities were $60,959, all of which fall due for payment within 
twelve months of the balance sheet date.&#160;&#160;The Company has minimal 
long-term commitments.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 90pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The carrying values of accounts payable and accrued liabilities
approximate their fair values due to the relatively short periods to maturity of
the instruments.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT:

DISPLAY: inline">NOTES TO THE FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</font></div>

<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new

<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Note 
14</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: 
inline">Capital Management</font></font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Company&#8217;s objectives when managing capital are to 
safeguard its ability to continue as a going concern, to provide an adequate 
return to shareholders, to meet external capital requirements on credit 
facilities and to support any growth plans.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The capital of the Company consists of the items included in 
shareholders&#8217; equity and cash net of debt obligations. The Company 
monitors capital based on the debt to debt-plus-equity ratio. Debt is total debt
shown on the balance sheet, less cash. Debt-plus-equity is calculated as debt 
shown on the balance sheet, plus total shareholders&#8217; equity which includes
share capital, warrants, contributed surplus and deficit. Currently the Company 
has no debt. The Company&#8217;s Board of Directors approves management&#8217;s 
annual capital expenditures plans and reviews and approves any material debt 
borrowing plans proposed by the Company&#8217;s management.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">As at December 31, 2015, the company had no externally imposed 
capital requirements nor were there any changes in the company&#8217;s approach 
to capital management during the year.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">Note 
15&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; 
DISPLAY: inline">Segmental Reporting</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
DISPLAY: inline">The Company has one reportable operating segment which is 
primarily the business of exploration and development of oil and gas and other 
mineral related opportunities, through companies in which the Company 
invests.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
36pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">1. I have reviewed this annual report on Form 20-F of FEC 
Resources Inc.;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
36pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">2. Based on my knowledge, this report does not contain any 
untrue statement of a material fact or omit to state a material fact necessary 
to make the statements made, in light of the circumstances under which such 
statements were made, not misleading with respect to the period covered by this 
report;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
36pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">3. Based on my knowledge, the financial statements, and other 
financial information included in this report, fairly present in all material 
respects the financial condition, results of operations and cash flows of the 
company as of, and for, the periods presented in this report;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 
36pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">4. The company&#8217;s other certifying officer and I are 
responsible for establishing and maintaining disclosure controls and procedures 
(as defined in Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(e) and 15d-15(e)) and internal control 
over financial reporting (as defined in Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(f) and 15d-
15(f)) for the company and have:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>
<div>

</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
DISPLAY: inline">Designed such disclosure controls and procedures, or caused 
such disclosure controls and procedures to be designed under our supervision, to
ensure that material information relating to the company, including its 
consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to us by others within those entities, 
particularly during the period in which this report is being

</td>

</td>

<div align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;

</td>
